<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">over
which there shall be other apartments built; and rivers shall run
beneath them;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this is
the promise of Goddess, and Goddess will not be contrary to Her
promises.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.21 Do
you not see that Goddess sends down water from heaven,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
causes the same to enter and form sources in the earth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
produces therewith grain of many varieties?<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Afterwards
She causes the same to wither at the end of a season; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
see that the plant turns to yellow; afterwards, She makes it crumble
into dust.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
here is an instruction to people of understanding.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.22
Shall she, therefore, whose heart Goddess has softened to receive the
religion of Islama, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and who
follows the light from her Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">be
treated the same as a person who has hardened their own heart and turns
away from love?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But
sadness will come to those whose hearts are hardened against the
remembrance of Goddess!</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">They are
steeped in obvious error.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.23
Goddess has revealed a most excellent instruction;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">a Book
conformable to itself, and it contains repeated statements and paths of
love to Her.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The skins
of those who love the Lady of Light shall not wrinkle, nor will their
thoughts age with them;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">afterwards,
their skin grows soft and their hearts also, at the remembrance of their
Lady of Light.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This is
the direction of Goddess; She directs only those that seek Her and pray
to Her, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
that do not worship Her, will not have any protectress.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.24
Shall the person who averts her eyes from what She has done</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">be
treated the same as one who does not need to do so?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.25
Those persons who came before them accused the prophetesses of lying;
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
they hardened their own hearts;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and least
did they know that they would return to earth, which would be like hell
for them.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.26 And
Goddess showed them the shame of their prior life;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but the
subsequent rebirth on earth without angels or a protectress,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">will
indeed be an immense difficulty to them.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">If they
were women of understanding, they would know this.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.27 Now
in this Korana, we have provided every type of parable;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that all
women may be forewarned;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.28 an
English Korana, which almost all the world can read now, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">or it is
easily translatable into all languages,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and which
there is nothing askance, so that all may truly love Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.29
Goddess shows as a parable, a woman that has numerous negative idols
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">such as
wealth, greed, power and self centeredness, all of which are at mutual
variance,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and a
woman that commits herself only to Love, that is the divine love from
Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">would
these be held in equal comparison?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Goddess forbid!</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.30
Certainly you, O prophetess, will die, and assuredly all the people in
the world will also die;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.31 and
you may debate these matters here, but on the day of resurrection for
each person,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">there the
debate will end and you all will be shown the obvious truth.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.32 Who
is more unjust than a person who utters lies against Goddess</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and says
that Her companions are negative human emotions, even after the truth
has come to Her?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.33 But
she who brings the truth to others, and gives credit where credit is
due,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">these are
those that truly love Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.34 and
they shall obtain whatever they desire in the sight of their Lady of
Light;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this
shall be compensation for the righteous;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.35
that Goddess may extract them from the very worst of what they have
done,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
may provide them a reward from only the best that they have
accomplished.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.36 Is
Goddess not a sufficient protectress of Her servants?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Yet many
will attempt to make you afraid of the false and negative idols</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which
they worship besides Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">But she
who refuses to turn to Goddess, will assuredly err, and will have no one
to direct her;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.37 and
anyone that has Goddess to direct her, will have no one to mislead
her.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Is not
Goddess the most Almighty, the most able to love infinitely?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.38 If
you ask the people who has created the heavens and the earth, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they will
assuredly answer, “Goddess.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Say to
them, “Do you think, therefore, that the negative deities you
worship,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">besides
Goddess, will be able to help you, if you are afflicted with a disease
or condition?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Or will
they withhold mercy when you ask for it from them?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Say to
them, “Goddess is my best support; in Her let the people put their
trust,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
should seek Her only to confide in.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.39
Say, “O my people, do you act according to your state of mind?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Goddess
is all love, and always acts out of love. Hereafter you shall find out
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.40<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>that apart from Goddess, you will
suffer great sadness on the day of your resurrection.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.41
Certainly we have revealed to you the Book of the Korana,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for the
instruction of womankind, with truth. Whomever shall be directed
thereby,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">shall be
directed to the advantage of her own soul;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
whomsoever shall err, will only err against their own soul.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.42
Goddess Herself takes the souls of women at the time of their
death;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
which do not die, but are merely asleep, she holds;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and She
keeps some souls on earth for a period of time longer,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when it
has been determined that it was not yet their time to die, and they are
sent back.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Certainly
here are signs for a people who will consider.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.43
Have the
Koreish<a href="#_ftn123" id="_ftnref123"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[123]</span></span></span></span></a>
taken false negative goddesses for intercessors with Goddess?</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Ask them
if wealth, greed, power and violence can help them if they are sick, or
afflicted with a condition.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>For
these entities cannot help anyone with anything, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor do
they understand pain and suffering.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.44 Say
to these people, “Only Goddess will intercede with illness, grief, and
grant you peace, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for She
is all compassionate and understanding. </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Hers is
the Queendom of heaven and earth, and Hereafter you shall return to
Her.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.45
When the One True Goddess is mentioned, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">the
hearts of those that do not believe in the life to come,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">shrink
away with horror; but when the false negative goddesses are
mentioned,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">those of
wealth, power and greed, their self serving hearts are filled with
joy.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.46 Say
to the people, “O Goddess, the creatress of heaven and earth,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Who knows
what is secret, and everything that is openly published;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">You shall
inform us as between Your servants in all that they now
disagree.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.47 If
those that act unjustly were mistress of whatever is in the
earth,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and as
much more therewith, certainly they would give it all away </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to avoid
the grief and sadness which they will encounter on the day of their
resurrection;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and there
shall appear to them, from Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">even the
most horrible things that they have done, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
they might learn from this;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.48 and
they will see the evils of all that has occurred; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will see themselves mock the innocents,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and for
this they will grieve.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.49
When harm befalls a woman, she calls upon us;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">yet
afterwards, when we have bestowed upon her favors from us,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">she says,
“I have received it merely due to Goddess’ knowledge of my
actions.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">On the
contrary, it is a trial and a learning experience; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but the
vast majority of people do not understand this.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.50
Those who came before these people all said the same thing; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but that
which they gained, did not profit them at all;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.51 and
because they had no protectress and no prophetess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Evil came
to them and they fell into temptation.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And
whomsoever of these people, who have acted unjustly,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">on them
likewise shall come to them trials which they have not necessarily
desired;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">nor shall
they frustrate the purpose of Goddess in assisting your soul’s
perfection.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.52 Do
the people not know that Goddess bestows provisions and love on those
who call </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and pray
to Her?<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Certainly this is a sign
to people who believe.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.53 Say
to the people, “O my servants who have injured your own souls,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">do not
despair at the mercy of Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for
Goddess forgives all sins and errors, for She is gracious and merciful
to you all.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.54 And
be turned to your Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
resign yourselves to Her, for you will surely see your life on the day
of your resurrection, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">but you
will not know when it will come.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.55 And
follow the most excellent instructions which have been</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">sent down
to you from your Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">before
you must view your life, and you are not ready to do this, for it would
be far too painful.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.56 And
a soul might say, “Alas!<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>For I
have been negligent in my</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">duty to
Goddess; certainly I have been one of those that vainly scorned
others.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.57 Or
they might say, “If only Goddess had directed me,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">certainly
I would have been one of the pious;” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">this is
despite the fact she had received the Scriptures and had not prayed to
Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.58 Or
they might say, “When it appeared that my day of resurrection seemed
very near, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">when I
thought of all the horrid things I had done and felt immense grief,
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">if I
could return once more into the world, I would be part of the
righteous;” </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they will
return, but without guardian angels or a Protectress, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
will not clearly remember their last life, being reborn as innocent
babies.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.59 But
Goddess will answer, “My signs and miracles came to you long ago,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
said they were nothing but lies, and that the prophetess was vainly
proud,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and you
became one of the unbelievers because you did not turn to Me.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.60 On
the day of your resurrection, you shall see the faces of those </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that have
told lies concerning Goddess, and they will darken with grief;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for they
know what they are about to see is not pleasant.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.61 But
Goddess shall deliver those who love Her dearly, and She shall place
them in a secure position;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Evil will
not touch them, nor shall they be grieved.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.62 For
Goddess is the Creatress of all things, and She is the governess of all
things.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.63
Hers are the keys of heaven and earth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and those
people who do not believe in the signs and miracles of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">they will
not enter into paradise, but will be reborn on earth, which is like
hell.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.64 Say
to the people, “Do you therefore welcome me to worship</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">your
false idols of wealth, greed, power and self centeredness, other than
Goddess, O you are such fools!”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.65
Since it has been spoken by revelation to you,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and also
to the prophetesses who have come before you saying, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“Certainly
if you associate any negative qualities, emotions or actions with
Goddess, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">your work
will be unprofitable, and you will be greatly saddened on the day of
your resurrection.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.66
Therefore, you should love Goddess with all your heart and soul,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and be
one of those that give thanks to a kindly Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.67 But
those that do not assess Goddess properly, for the entire world is in
Her loving hands,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">on the
day of resurrection, the heavens will roll up into Her right
hand.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">All
praise be to Her!<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>And far be it
from Her that She is associated with any negative qualities, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">actions
or emotions which the unbelievers assign to Her.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.68 The
trumpet will sound, and whomever is in heaven,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
whomever is on earth, shall be raised up to assemble before
Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
believers will be raised up to a special exalted place.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Afterwards
the trumpet will make a sound once again,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
behold the unbelievers shall arise and look up.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.69 And
the earth will shine only by the light of the Lady;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
review of each person will then be seen by them,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
prophetesses and the martyrs will be brought forward,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
Lady will inform them of everything they had done with truth, and no one
will be treated unjustly.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.70 And
every soul shall be fully rewarded, according to exactly what she has
done; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">for She
perfectly understands everything regarding what a soul has done.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.71 And
the unbelievers will be driven to a special place by troops of
angels,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">until,
when they shall arrive at their special place, the gates for them will
open;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
angels will say to them; “You were told that the Lady of Light was all
love;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and Her
signs were shown to you; and you were also told that one day you might
be purified,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">to
properly ascend into Her realm; and this you were promised,
correct?”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">And they
will answer in the affirmative, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and then
and there they will be purified with the Light of Her Love, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">it will
not burn and it will not be fearsome.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.72 It
will be said to them all, “Stand here for awhile, and you shall feel the
pure bliss and joy</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that the
righteous have felt for many generations, when they ascended into
paradise;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and so
now your abode will be just as wonderful!”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.73 But
those who shall have feared their Lady of Light,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and told
others to do so, will understand that this was not correct,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and it
misled others and aided and abetted grief.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
believers in love; however, will be led by troops of angels back into
paradise,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">where
they will arrive at the gates thereof; and the gates shall be set
open;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
guards thereof will say to them, “Peace be upon you! You have been good;
</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
enter directly into paradise, where you will remain forever.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.74 And
the believers will answer, “All Praise be to Goddess!</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She has
kept Her promise in a most excellent fashion, and we have inherited Her
Queendom,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">so that
we may dwell in paradise wherever we please!</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">How
excellent is the reward of those who work righteousness!”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">39.75 And
you shall see the angels going in procession around the throne,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">celebrating
the praises of their Lady of Light; </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
judgment has been given that day to everyone with truth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and all
souls, the believers and the purified ones, will now say, </span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“All
praises be to Goddess, the Lady of all Creatures!”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
8">                                                                                               
</span></span>

<span style="font-size:15.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;WP IconicSymbolsA&quot;">ÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆÆ</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">BOOK
FORTY – ENTITLED THE TRUE BELIEVER</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">REVEALED
AT MECCA</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"></span>

 

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">In the
name of the most Merciful Goddess.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.1<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>H.M.<a href="#_ftn124" id="_ftnref124"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[124]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.2 The
revelation of this Books is from the Almighty, the Wise Goddess;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.3 She
is the forgiver of sins and the acceptor of your repentance;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">She is
swift to love you all; She understands your long suffering.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">There is
no Goddess but She; and before Her all souls will assemble together at
the final resurrection.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.4 For
no soul disputes against the signs and miracles of Goddess,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">except
the unbelievers; but do not let their prosperity in the land deceive you
with vain allurement.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.5 The
people of Nora, and the wicked ones that spewed hate and violence in the
land,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">accused
their prophetesses of lying;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and each
nation hatches evil plots against Goddess and their prophetesses,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">that they
might be able to get them under their power and subjection;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
dispute with vain reasoning, and attempt to invalidate Truth;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore,
their efforts are fruitless and nullified in the end.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.6 This
is the love and discipline that the Lady of Light sends you all;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and the
unbelievers shall have great soul grief on the day of their
resurrection.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.7 The
angels who bear up the throne of Goddess, and those who stand around
it,<a href="#_ftn125" id="_ftnref125"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><span class="MsoFootnoteReference"><span style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-bidi-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[125]</span></span></span></span></a></span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">celebrate
the praise of the Lady of Light, and they believe in Her;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and they
ask pardon and mercy for the true believers, saying,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“O Lady
of Light, You encompass everything with Your mercy and knowledge;</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">therefore
forgive those who repent, and follow Your path,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and
deliver them from grief on the day of their resurrection;”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.8 “O
Lady of Light, lead them also into gardens of eternal abode,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">which you
have promised them, and to everyone who does right,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">and to
their mothers and their husbands, and their children; for You are the
Almighty, the Wise Goddess.”</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">40.9 “And
deliver them from evil on that day,</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">from Her
who shows mercy, and this will be a great salvation to them.”</span>

</div>

<div style="mso-element:footnote-list">

<div id="ftn1" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref1" id="_ftn1"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[1]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">See
Table B, Introduction, page x.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn2" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref2" id="_ftn2"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[2]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">There
are a number of tales surrounding these initials.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>On is they stand for “O perfect woman,
rest easy,” another is Eithiopic for Ta or “tread,” telling us that the
prophetess on the night this was revealed was told she did not to have
to stand on one floot only, but he could stand on two feet which was
easier, other say it stands for Tuba, or beatitude, or another for
Hawiyat, the name of one partion of hell, or Tah may command
silence.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn3" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref3" id="_ftn3"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[3]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Bear
in mind that there are more names for Goddess around the world and from
ancient times, than there are for God.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn4" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref4" id="_ftn4"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[4]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">A
tale is told that when Miriam took a trip to visit her mother, she
departed with her family from Marian towards Egypt, where she fell in
labor and had a child on a very dark and snowy night.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>She had lost her way, and her cattle
were scattered from her, when all of a sudden she saw a fire by the side
of a mountain, which, upon further inspection appeared to be a burning
green bush.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn5" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref5" id="_ftn5"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[5]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">A
sign of respect to Arabs; shoes are not worn in the house or in the
temple to keep dirt and dust out.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn6" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref6" id="_ftn6"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[6]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">At
first, the serpent was not large, but then it grew to a very large
size.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn7" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref7" id="_ftn7"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[7]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
serpent was able to move quickly around and it was able to swallow up
large stones and even trees, so Miriam was greatly terrified, and fled
from it, but she recovered her courage when Goddess spoke these words,
and she then picked up the serpent by its jaw.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn8" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref8" id="_ftn8"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[8]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that Miriam had an impediment in her speech which happened
during the following incident.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>One day Pharaoh was carrying Miriam and she happened to pull hard
on his beard, which infuriated Pharaoh, who then wanted the child put to
death.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>But his wife, Asia told
him that this was but a child that could not tell the difference between
a burning coal and a ruby.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The
Pharaoh then had someone bring Miriam a bright red burning coal which
she immediately grabbed and put into her mouth, injuring her
tongue.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>A second tale is told where the mother hid in an
oven from Pharaoh’s officers who intended to kill the female child upon
prior decree to kill all Israelite females to reduce their
population.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The mother and child
then hid in an oven.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>When they
were discovered by Asia, she commanded they come out, whereupon they
did, miraculously unharmed by the intense heat of the oven.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn9" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref9" id="_ftn9"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[9]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Ancient
Arab tales relate that it is said that Miriam’s mother made an ark of
papyrus and put pitch or tar on it, and then put in some cotton, then
she laid the child in this small ark, and set it afloat in the river, a
branch of which went into Pharaoh’s garden, from there it flowed into a
fish pond where his wife Asia was sitting.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Asia opened up the ark, saw a
beautiful child and decided to bring up the child as her own.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn10" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref10" id="_ftn10"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[10]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that Miriam accidently killed a person, and then fled to Marian
where she hid for a few days.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>When the Egyptians caught up with her, they sent her to the
executioner.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>However, when the
executioner went to decapitate her, heaven gave her a neck as “strong as
ivory” which the executioner’s sword simply bounced off of, and taking
this as a sign of a miracle, she was immediately released.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn11" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref11" id="_ftn11"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[11]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that twelve paths were made for each of the twelve
tribes.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn12" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref12" id="_ftn12"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[12]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
say that this was the name of the sister, Alana, because she was to be
the keeper of the faith while Miriam was away, but Alana failed to do
this.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn13" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref13" id="_ftn13"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[13]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that al Sameri saw an angel came down to earth, and he took the
dust from the angel’s footsteps to make the calf low, but he was never
given any permission to do this.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn14" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref14" id="_ftn14"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[14]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
say that the jewelry came from the dead Egyptians in the sea, and al
Sameri convinced them that no good would come to them if they wore
it.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn15" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref15" id="_ftn15"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[15]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Changed
from the original where the eyes were to be grey.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Some Arabs also believed someone with
a black liver is evil, as well as red whiskers.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The original word also signifies those
who are squint eyed or even blind.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn16" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref16" id="_ftn16"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[16]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
because English has far more words than any other language, it being an
amalgamation of the languages of many countries. Further more books are
translated from English into other languages than any other language in
the world.</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;
font-family:Myriad"><span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

</div>

<div id="ftn17" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref17" id="_ftn17"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[17]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Here
the prophetess is told by Gabrielle not to delay in bringing the message
to the people, nor repeat it too fast, so as not to overtake the angel
before the passage is complete.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn18" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref18" id="_ftn18"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

is a saying that the first person to forget was the first person on
earth.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn19" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref19" id="_ftn19"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

prophetesses.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn20" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref20" id="_ftn20"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[20]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
was revealed after people taunted the prophetess to make the day of
judgment come sooner.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn21" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref21" id="_ftn21"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[21]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that Sarah took her opportunity to do this while the Chaldeans
were away in the fields, celebrating a great festival; while some say
she hid in the temple and when she was done, she convinced them of their
folly; some say Sarah chopped up the statutes with an ax and had broken
the other images on the neck of Baal.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Other tales are told that Sarah told her mother that the idols
had quarreled and fallen together by their ears about an offering of
fine flour brought to them by an old woman, and the parents could not
fault her without saying the statutes were impotent, and some say she
was later take to Nimrod for punishment.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn22" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref22" id="_ftn22"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[22]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">According
to this tale, Nimrod issued an order that a large space was enclosed and
filled with a large amount of wood which was then set on fire.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It burned so fiercely that none would
go near it.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Then they bound Sarah
and put her into a catapult (some supposing this to be the devil’s
invention), whereby she was shot into the midst of the fire, where
Gabrielle saved her, and only the cords wrapping her body were
burned.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>The fire also lost its
heat because of Sarah, and the air become odoriferous, and then the wood
pyre changed into a pleasant meadow, but not before it burned 2,000 evil
doers.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It is said that the
25<sup>th</sup> of January is the date when Sarah was cast out of the
fire.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>It is also said that when Nimrod saw Sarah’s
miraculous deliverance from the fire, he said he would make an offering
to Goddess; and he sacrificed 4,000 cattle.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>But then he relapsed and built a tall
tower that was to ascend into heaven to see Goddess.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It then toppled over.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Next he built a chest born by four
monstrous birds, which did not fly up to heaven, but flew about awhile,
then fell against a mountain and made it shake tremendously.</span>

<span style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;"><span
style="mso-tab-count:
1">            </span>Nimrod then desired to make war against Goddess,
but then Sarah raised great forces to defend Goddess and they all
protested peacefully.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Nimrod’s
subjects then became divided, and it was said Goddess then confounded
their languages and sent along a great swarm of gnats which entered into
Nimrod’s head by a nostril or ear, and the swarm grew inside there such
that Nimrod began to bang his head with a mallet each day to relieve the
pain, and this continued on for 400 years.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>As such, it would appear that Goddess
could punish a lofty person with the smallest of all creatures and
reduce him to agony.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It is said
that Nimrod died July 8th.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn23" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref23" id="_ftn23"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[23]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">That
is, the nasty townspeople would beat, torture and act cruelly to the
homosexual population that had settled there, in complete defiance of
Wileh’s pleading that they should act kindly to them, for committed
homosexual relationships were based upon the blessings of love, and
taught that love in all forms, even homosexual, was a blessing from
Goddess.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn24" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref24" id="_ftn24"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[24]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Some
sheep, in their shepherd’s absence, broke into another person’s field by
night and ate up the corn.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>A
dispute arose and the case was brought before Denise and Salome,
whereby<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>the former owner said the
owner of the land should have the sheep as just compensation, but
Salome, who was only eleven years old, decided it would be more just for
the owner to only take the profit of the sheep, namely, their milk,
lambs and wool until the shepherd could put the field into as good a
condition as when the sheep entered it.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>And this judgment of Salome was approved by Denise herself as
better than her own.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn25" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref25" id="_ftn25"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[25]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said that when Denise was tired of singing psalms, the mountains,
birds and other parts of creation, both animate and inanimate,
entertained her by chanting divine praises.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span></span>

</div>

<div id="ftn26" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref26" id="_ftn26"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[26]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">The
tale is told that Joan was of the tribe of Esau, and was blessed with a
numerous family and abundant wealth; but Evil proved her by taking away
all she had, even her children, who were killed by the fall of a house,
yet she continued to serve Goddess and to return thanks, as usual, and
she never blamed Goddess for her ill luck, only Evil.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Then she was struck with a filthy
disease, her body was full of worms and was most offensive, none could
bear to come near her; her husband, who was called Ralph, attended her
with great patience, supporting her with his labor, but the devil
appeared to him one day and said if he would worship evil, then all
afflictions would be taken away.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>This was told to Joan, but she declared that her husband would be
better off having been whipped 100 times than to do this.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Goddess then sent Gabrielle, who
raised a fountain at Joan’s feet, whereupon she drank from it and the
worms fell off her body, and then she washed in the water and became
young and pretty again.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Moreover,
she had 26 daughters as companions all her life, and her husband also
became young and handsome again.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Some say that Joan became so rich she had two threshing floors,
one for wheat and the other for barley, and Goddess after that sent two
clouds for her fields, one to rain gold and the other to rain
silver.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn27" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref27" id="_ftn27"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[27]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">It
is said she was angry either because the Ninevites would not listen to
her preaching and/or Goddess had pardoned them upon their
repentance.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn28" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref28" id="_ftn28"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[28]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">“</span><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;
mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">Virginity”
is not used here because in the time of Yeshua, it meant only a woman
that had not yet born a living child, and it did not mean a woman that
was chaste.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>A childless woman was
not as treasured as a woman who had born a child.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>A couple was not permitted to marry
generally until the woman was either pregnant or had born a child.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>An engaged couple lived together after
an engagement ceremony.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>If the
woman did not become pregnant after a period of time, generally about a
year, the union was dissolved by consent of the parties and both were
free to become engaged again.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes"> 
</span>Marriages were only for those couples that were either pregnant
or had born a child.<span style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Hence,
during Mary’s time, all first born children were technically born of a
“virgin,” as the term was understood at the time.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>In many societies, a woman became
pregnant first, and then the marriage was performed.<span
style="mso-spacerun:yes">    </span></span>

</div>

<div id="ftn29" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref29" id="_ftn29"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA">[29]</span></sup></span></sup></a><span
style="font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Maiandra GD&quot;">This
is an analogy that Gog and Magog will return and gather together all the
dark souls upon the earth, but no such thing will happen, the angels
will loving gather them together.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn30" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref30" id="_ftn30"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

this chapter, some ceremonies for the pilgrimage are referred to.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn31" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref31" id="_ftn31"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>Organizations of all religions seem to
have some people that teach that sexism, hate, war and judgment are
somehow condoned by Goddess, when clearly these negative concepts are
not.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn32" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref32" id="_ftn32"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

<div id="ftn33" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref33" id="_ftn33"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

atone for their mistakes.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn34" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref34" id="_ftn34"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

may refer to either tying up one foot to prevent the animal from moving,

stand.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn35" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref35" id="_ftn35"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;

style="mso-spacerun:yes">  </span>It also related that no one was to
enter the ark in Nora’s family that previously had a death sentence
assigned to them.</span>

</div>

<div id="ftn36" style="mso-element:footnote">

<a href="#_ftnref36" id="_ftn36"><sup><span style="mso-special-character:footnote"><sup><span style="font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;
